We were able to disburse as much cash as the customers wanted.\u201d ',  During the discussion about Ujjivan\u2019s SFB transition, he said, \u201cWe have to provide the customers easy access; banking offered should be free of paperwork. We can open an account in five minutes if customers have Aadhar card. Today, technology enables us to do that and we can bring banking to every customer\u2019s doorstep."
